							<div class="heroRegionContent expandable">
								<div class="wrap" style="position: relative; overflow: hidden;">
									Based on total listings, Texas has the most land for sale on Lands of America. It also features the most acres for sale. Recent data from Lands of America records about $31 billion in land, homesites and other rural acreage for sale in the Lone Star State. This covers over 5,168,000 acres of land for sale in the state. Of the 254 counties in the state, <a href="https://www.landsofamerica.com/Comal-County-TX/all-land/">Comal County</a> had the most land and farms for sale. Based on comps submitted through the Lands of America Comparable Sales program last month, Texas had the most land sales. Of the 572 recorded land sales, the total value of all completed sales was $245 million for all property and land sold in Texas (a substantial change over the previous month). Edwards County had the most land sales recently in the state. The Lone Star State has over 200 public hunting areas, which include wildlife management areas, state parks, and U.S. Forest Service lands. The state is also home to 191, 000 miles of rivers and streams, along with numerous lakes and reservoirs, and Gulf of Mexico coastline. Texas is the second-biggest state in the United States, covering an area of 268,601 square miles (172 million acres). Of this area, 261,232 square miles of the state is land, while the remaining 7,365 square miles is covered by water. As one the nation's top agricultural states, current uses of land for sale in Texas include for agriculture, hunting, fishing, and residential use. Livestock on farms and ranches for sale in Texas include cattle, horses, goats, sheep, and pigs. Game species to be found on land for sale in Texas include whitetail deer, dove, hog, turkey, and quail. Fishermen have their choice of bass, catfish, trout, pike, walleye, and salmon.

				<div class="sidebarGeoContent expandable" style="margin-bottom: 1em; margin-top: 1em;">
					<h4>Bosque County Land Info</h4>
					<div class="wrap" style="position: relative; overflow: hidden;">Bosque County, Texas, is considered a non-metropolitan area located in proximity to a large metro region. The county is the 131st largest county in the state based on population and it's the 81st largest based on size (1,003 square miles).  The most common type of land for sale in Bosque County is farms. Other common property types for sale in Bosque County include ranches, residential property, recreational property and lakefront property. Recent Lands of Texas data showed 30,031 acres of land for sale in Bosque County valued at a combined $147 million, with a median sale price of $151,950. Based on data for median land prices throughout the state, land for sale in Bosque County is currently valued cheaper than in other counties.  The city of Clifton in Bosque County featured the most land listings for sale. The average price-per-acre value of land for sale in Bosque County places the county 100th overall in the state. Bosque County is located in Central Texas, a region comprising 30 counties. The central region of Texas covers the state's three largest cities: Houston, Dallas-Fort Worth and San Antonio. The limestone terrain of Texas Hill Country lies in Central Texas, as do the state's three largest rivers, the Trinity, the Brazos and the Colorado.The value and availability of land, make Bosque County a popular destination for older snowbirds. With its farm sector generating estimated annual receipts of $78 million, Bosque County farms and ranches are mostly focused on cattle and other livestock such as sheep, goats and horses.</div>

<script type="text/javascript">
				var justSetState = false;
				/**/
				window.onpopstate = function(event) {
					updateFromHistory();
				};

				function updateFromHistory() {
					if (history.state && !justSetState) {
						if (history.state.filterDisplay) {
							stopFilterListeners();
							setFilterValue(history.state.filterDisplay, true, false);
							startFilterListeners()
						}
						if (history.state.filter) {
							updateSearchFilter(history.state.filter, true, false, true);
						}
						else {
							/**/
						}
						if ((history.state.pagingInfo) && (!($.isEmptyObject(history.state.pagingInfo)))) {
							updateResultsPagingData(history.state.pagingInfo.pagingData, history.state.pagingInfo.baseurl);
						}
					}
					else {
						// no state saved, should load normally, right?
					}
					justSetState = false;
				}


				/**/

				$(document).ready(function() {
					updateFromHistory();
					lazyload();
					$('.showcase-desc').trunk8({lines:3, tooltip:false});

					$('.premium-desc').trunk8({lines:2, tooltip:false});
					$('.basic-desc').trunk8({lines:2, tooltip:false});
					$(window).resize(function () {
						$('.showcase-desc').trunk8({lines:3, tooltip:false});
						$('.premium-desc').trunk8({lines:2, tooltip:false});
						$('.basic-desc').trunk8({lines:2, tooltip:false});
					});

					if ((!bIsIE) && ($.isEmptyObject(history.state))) {
						justSetState = true;
						/**/
						var pagingInfo = { pagingData: {CURRENTPAGE: '1', STARTPAGELINKS: '1', ENDPAGELINKS: '10', PAGECOUNT: '20'}, baseurl: "/Bosque-County-TX/all-land/50-5000-acres/is-active/is-under-contract/is-inactive/is-sold/no-house/" };
						/**/
						var newHS = { filter: convertKeysToLower(getSearchFromPage()), loaurl: '/Bosque-County-TX/all-land/50-5000-acres/is-active/is-under-contract/is-inactive/is-sold/no-house/', filterDisplay: getFilterValues(), pagingInfo: pagingInfo };
						/**/
						history.replaceState(newHS, null, '/Bosque-County-TX/all-land/50-5000-acres/is-active/is-under-contract/is-inactive/is-sold/no-house/');
					}


					resetExpandables(".expandable");
				});

				function resetExpandables(selectorVal) {
					/*  */

					$(selectorVal).each(function(index) {
					var slideHeight = 250;
					    if ($(selectorVal).attr('class').split(' ')[index]=='heroRegionContent'){
					    		slideHeight=103;
					    };
					    var $this = $(this);
					    var $wrap = $this.children(".wrap");
					    var defHeight = $wrap.height();
					    if (defHeight >= slideHeight) {
					        var $readMore = $this.find(".read-more");
					        $wrap.css("height", slideHeight + "px");
					        $readMore.append("<a href='#'>More +</a>");
					        $readMore.children("a").bind("click", function(event) {
					            var curHeight = $wrap.height();
					            if (curHeight == slideHeight) {
					                $wrap.animate({
					                    height: defHeight
					                }, "normal");
					                $(this).text("Less -");
					                $readMore.children(".elipses").hide();
					                // $wrap.children(".gradient").fadeOut();
					            } else {
					                $wrap.animate({
					                    height: slideHeight
					                }, "normal");
					                $(this).text("More +");
					                $readMore.children(".elipses").show();
					                // $wrap.children(".gradient").fadeIn();
					            }
					            return false;
					        });
					    } else {
					    	$this.find(".read-more").hide();
					    }
					});

				}


			</script>

			{{/if}}

									Based on total listings, Texas has the most land for sale on Lands of America. It also features the most acres for sale. Recent data from Lands of America records about $31 billion in land, homesites and other rural acreage for sale in the Lone Star State. This covers over 5,168,000 acres of land for sale in the state. Of the 254 counties in the state, <a href="https://www.landsofamerica.com/Comal-County-TX/all-land/">Comal County</a> had the most land and farms for sale. Based on comps submitted through the Lands of America Comparable Sales program last month, Texas had the most land sales. Of the 572 recorded land sales, the total value of all completed sales was $245 million for all property and land sold in Texas (a substantial change over the previous month). Edwards County had the most land sales recently in the state. The Lone Star State has over 200 public hunting areas, which include wildlife management areas, state parks, and U.S. Forest Service lands. The state is also home to 191, 000 miles of rivers and streams, along with numerous lakes and reservoirs, and Gulf of Mexico coastline. Texas is the second-biggest state in the United States, covering an area of 268,601 square miles (172 million acres). Of this area, 261,232 square miles of the state is land, while the remaining 7,365 square miles is covered by water. As one the nation's top agricultural states, current uses of land for sale in Texas include for agriculture, hunting, fishing, and residential use. Livestock on farms and ranches for sale in Texas include cattle, horses, goats, sheep, and pigs. Game species to be found on land for sale in Texas include whitetail deer, dove, hog, turkey, and quail. Fishermen have their choice of bass, catfish, trout, pike, walleye, and salmon.

Bosque Lake Ranch is a recreational ranch located only 60 miles from Fort Worth, TX. It is located on the Somervell-Bosque county line. The property has 3,600 feet of Texas State Highway 144 frontage and 3,100 feet of County Road 2720 frontage.

<script type="text/javascript">
				var justSetState = false;
				/**/
				window.onpopstate = function(event) {
					updateFromHistory();
				};

				function updateFromHistory() {
					if (history.state && !justSetState) {
						if (history.state.filterDisplay) {
							stopFilterListeners();
							setFilterValue(history.state.filterDisplay, true, false);
							startFilterListeners()
						}
						if (history.state.filter) {
							updateSearchFilter(history.state.filter, true, false, true);
						}
						else {
							/**/
						}
						if ((history.state.pagingInfo) && (!($.isEmptyObject(history.state.pagingInfo)))) {
							updateResultsPagingData(history.state.pagingInfo.pagingData, history.state.pagingInfo.baseurl);
						}
					}
					else {
						// no state saved, should load normally, right?
					}
					justSetState = false;
				}


				/**/

				$(document).ready(function() {
					updateFromHistory();
					lazyload();
					$('.showcase-desc').trunk8({lines:3, tooltip:false});

					$('.premium-desc').trunk8({lines:2, tooltip:false});
					$('.basic-desc').trunk8({lines:2, tooltip:false});
					$(window).resize(function () {
						$('.showcase-desc').trunk8({lines:3, tooltip:false});
						$('.premium-desc').trunk8({lines:2, tooltip:false});
						$('.basic-desc').trunk8({lines:2, tooltip:false});
					});

					if ((!bIsIE) && ($.isEmptyObject(history.state))) {
						justSetState = true;
						/**/
						var pagingInfo = { pagingData: {CURRENTPAGE: '2', STARTPAGELINKS: '1', ENDPAGELINKS: '10', PAGECOUNT: '20'}, baseurl: "/Bosque-County-TX/all-land/50-5000-acres/is-active/is-under-contract/is-inactive/is-sold/no-house/" };
						/**/
						var newHS = { filter: convertKeysToLower(getSearchFromPage()), loaurl: '/Bosque-County-TX/all-land/50-5000-acres/is-active/is-under-contract/is-inactive/is-sold/no-house/page-2/', filterDisplay: getFilterValues(), pagingInfo: pagingInfo };
						/**/
						history.replaceState(newHS, null, '/Bosque-County-TX/all-land/50-5000-acres/is-active/is-under-contract/is-inactive/is-sold/no-house/page-2/');
					}


					resetExpandables(".expandable");
				});

				function resetExpandables(selectorVal) {
					/*  */

					$(selectorVal).each(function(index) {
					var slideHeight = 250;
					    if ($(selectorVal).attr('class').split(' ')[index]=='heroRegionContent'){
					    		slideHeight=103;
					    };
					    var $this = $(this);
					    var $wrap = $this.children(".wrap");
					    var defHeight = $wrap.height();
					    if (defHeight >= slideHeight) {
					        var $readMore = $this.find(".read-more");
					        $wrap.css("height", slideHeight + "px");
					        $readMore.append("<a href='#'>More +</a>");
					        $readMore.children("a").bind("click", function(event) {
					            var curHeight = $wrap.height();
					            if (curHeight == slideHeight) {
					                $wrap.animate({
					                    height: defHeight
					                }, "normal");
					                $(this).text("Less -");
					                $readMore.children(".elipses").hide();
					                // $wrap.children(".gradient").fadeOut();
					            } else {
					                $wrap.animate({
					                    height: slideHeight
					                }, "normal");
					                $(this).text("More +");
					                $readMore.children(".elipses").show();
					                // $wrap.children(".gradient").fadeIn();
					            }
					            return false;
					        });
					    } else {
					    	$this.find(".read-more").hide();
					    }
					});

				}


			</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
					// SearchBar Stick Top Nav
					var stickyNavTop;
					$(document).ready(function() {
						if( $('.search-nav').length ){
							updateStickyNavTop();
							var stickyNav = function(){
								var scrollTop = $(window).scrollTop();
								if (scrollTop > stickyNavTop) { $('.search-nav').addClass('sticky'); }
								else { $('.search-nav').removeClass('sticky'); }
							};
							stickyNav();
							$(window).scroll(function() { stickyNav(); });
						}

					});

					function updateStickyNavTop() {
						stickyNavTop = $('.search-nav').offset().top;
					}

								<div class="wrap" style="position: relative; overflow: hidden;">
									Based on total listings, Texas has the most land for sale on Lands of America. It also features the most acres for sale. Recent data from Lands of America records about $31 billion in land, homesites and other rural acreage for sale in the Lone Star State. This covers over 5,168,000 acres of land for sale in the state. Of the 254 counties in the state, <a href="https://www.landsofamerica.com/Comal-County-TX/all-land/">Comal County</a> had the most land and farms for sale. Based on comps submitted through the Lands of America Comparable Sales program last month, Texas had the most land sales. Of the 572 recorded land sales, the total value of all completed sales was $245 million for all property and land sold in Texas (a substantial change over the previous month). Edwards County had the most land sales recently in the state. The Lone Star State has over 200 public hunting areas, which include wildlife management areas, state parks, and U.S. Forest Service lands. The state is also home to 191, 000 miles of rivers and streams, along with numerous lakes and reservoirs, and Gulf of Mexico coastline. Texas is the second-biggest state in the United States, covering an area of 268,601 square miles (172 million acres). Of this area, 261,232 square miles of the state is land, while the remaining 7,365 square miles is covered by water. As one the nation's top agricultural states, current uses of land for sale in Texas include for agriculture, hunting, fishing, and residential use. Livestock on farms and ranches for sale in Texas include cattle, horses, goats, sheep, and pigs. Game species to be found on land for sale in Texas include whitetail deer, dove, hog, turkey, and quail. Fishermen have their choice of bass, catfish, trout, pike, walleye, and salmon.

<script type="text/javascript">
				var justSetState = false;
				/**/
				window.onpopstate = function(event) {
					updateFromHistory();
				};

				function updateFromHistory() {
					if (history.state && !justSetState) {
						if (history.state.filterDisplay) {
							stopFilterListeners();
							setFilterValue(history.state.filterDisplay, true, false);
							startFilterListeners()
						}
						if (history.state.filter) {
							updateSearchFilter(history.state.filter, true, false, true);
						}
						else {
							/**/
						}
						if ((history.state.pagingInfo) && (!($.isEmptyObject(history.state.pagingInfo)))) {
							updateResultsPagingData(history.state.pagingInfo.pagingData, history.state.pagingInfo.baseurl);
						}
					}
					else {
						// no state saved, should load normally, right?
					}
					justSetState = false;
				}


				/**/

				$(document).ready(function() {
					updateFromHistory();
					lazyload();
					$('.showcase-desc').trunk8({lines:3, tooltip:false});

					$('.premium-desc').trunk8({lines:2, tooltip:false});
					$('.basic-desc').trunk8({lines:2, tooltip:false});
					$(window).resize(function () {
						$('.showcase-desc').trunk8({lines:3, tooltip:false});
						$('.premium-desc').trunk8({lines:2, tooltip:false});
						$('.basic-desc').trunk8({lines:2, tooltip:false});
					});

					if ((!bIsIE) && ($.isEmptyObject(history.state))) {
						justSetState = true;
						/**/
						var pagingInfo = { pagingData: {CURRENTPAGE: '3', STARTPAGELINKS: '1', ENDPAGELINKS: '10', PAGECOUNT: '20'}, baseurl: "/Bosque-County-TX/all-land/50-5000-acres/is-active/is-under-contract/is-inactive/is-sold/no-house/" };
						/**/
						var newHS = { filter: convertKeysToLower(getSearchFromPage()), loaurl: '/Bosque-County-TX/all-land/50-5000-acres/is-active/is-under-contract/is-inactive/is-sold/no-house/page-3/', filterDisplay: getFilterValues(), pagingInfo: pagingInfo };
						/**/
						history.replaceState(newHS, null, '/Bosque-County-TX/all-land/50-5000-acres/is-active/is-under-contract/is-inactive/is-sold/no-house/page-3/');
					}


					resetExpandables(".expandable");
				});

				function resetExpandables(selectorVal) {
					/*  */

					$(selectorVal).each(function(index) {
					var slideHeight = 250;
					    if ($(selectorVal).attr('class').split(' ')[index]=='heroRegionContent'){
					    		slideHeight=103;
					    };
					    var $this = $(this);
					    var $wrap = $this.children(".wrap");
					    var defHeight = $wrap.height();
					    if (defHeight >= slideHeight) {
					        var $readMore = $this.find(".read-more");
					        $wrap.css("height", slideHeight + "px");
					        $readMore.append("<a href='#'>More +</a>");
					        $readMore.children("a").bind("click", function(event) {
					            var curHeight = $wrap.height();
					            if (curHeight == slideHeight) {
					                $wrap.animate({
					                    height: defHeight
					                }, "normal");
					                $(this).text("Less -");
					                $readMore.children(".elipses").hide();
					                // $wrap.children(".gradient").fadeOut();
					            } else {
					                $wrap.animate({
					                    height: slideHeight
					                }, "normal");
					                $(this).text("More +");
					                $readMore.children(".elipses").show();
					                // $wrap.children(".gradient").fadeIn();
					            }
					            return false;
					        });
					    } else {
					    	$this.find(".read-more").hide();
					    }
					});

				}


			</script>

							<div class="heroRegionContent expandable">
								<div class="wrap" style="position: relative; overflow: hidden;">
									Based on total listings, Texas has the most land for sale on Lands of America. It also features the most acres for sale. Recent data from Lands of America records about $31 billion in land, homesites and other rural acreage for sale in the Lone Star State. This covers over 5,168,000 acres of land for sale in the state. Of the 254 counties in the state, <a href="https://www.landsofamerica.com/Comal-County-TX/all-land/">Comal County</a> had the most land and farms for sale. Based on comps submitted through the Lands of America Comparable Sales program last month, Texas had the most land sales. Of the 572 recorded land sales, the total value of all completed sales was $245 million for all property and land sold in Texas (a substantial change over the previous month). Edwards County had the most land sales recently in the state. The Lone Star State has over 200 public hunting areas, which include wildlife management areas, state parks, and U.S. Forest Service lands. The state is also home to 191, 000 miles of rivers and streams, along with numerous lakes and reservoirs, and Gulf of Mexico coastline. Texas is the second-biggest state in the United States, covering an area of 268,601 square miles (172 million acres). Of this area, 261,232 square miles of the state is land, while the remaining 7,365 square miles is covered by water. As one the nation's top agricultural states, current uses of land for sale in Texas include for agriculture, hunting, fishing, and residential use. Livestock on farms and ranches for sale in Texas include cattle, horses, goats, sheep, and pigs. Game species to be found on land for sale in Texas include whitetail deer, dove, hog, turkey, and quail. Fishermen have their choice of bass, catfish, trout, pike, walleye, and salmon.

				var justSetState = false;
				/**/
				window.onpopstate = function(event) {
					updateFromHistory();
				};

				function updateFromHistory() {
					if (history.state && !justSetState) {
						if (history.state.filterDisplay) {
							stopFilterListeners();
							setFilterValue(history.state.filterDisplay, true, false);
							startFilterListeners()
						}
						if (history.state.filter) {
							updateSearchFilter(history.state.filter, true, false, true);
						}
						else {
							/**/
						}
						if ((history.state.pagingInfo) && (!($.isEmptyObject(history.state.pagingInfo)))) {
							updateResultsPagingData(history.state.pagingInfo.pagingData, history.state.pagingInfo.baseurl);
						}
					}
					else {
						// no state saved, should load normally, right?
					}
					justSetState = false;
				}

					updateFromHistory();
					lazyload();

					$('.premium-desc').trunk8({lines:2, tooltip:false});
					$('.basic-desc').trunk8({lines:2, tooltip:false});
					$(window).resize(function () {
						$('.showcase-desc').trunk8({lines:3, tooltip:false});
						$('.premium-desc').trunk8({lines:2, tooltip:false});
						$('.basic-desc').trunk8({lines:2, tooltip:false});
					});

					if ((!bIsIE) && ($.isEmptyObject(history.state))) {
						justSetState = true;
						/**/
						var pagingInfo = { pagingData: {CURRENTPAGE: '4', STARTPAGELINKS: '1', ENDPAGELINKS: '10', PAGECOUNT: '20'}, baseurl: "/Bosque-County-TX/all-land/50-5000-acres/is-active/is-under-contract/is-inactive/is-sold/no-house/" };
						/**/
						var newHS = { filter: convertKeysToLower(getSearchFromPage()), loaurl: '/Bosque-County-TX/all-land/50-5000-acres/is-active/is-under-contract/is-inactive/is-sold/no-house/page-4/', filterDisplay: getFilterValues(), pagingInfo: pagingInfo };

						history.replaceState(newHS, null, '/Bosque-County-TX/all-land/50-5000-acres/is-active/is-under-contract/is-inactive/is-sold/no-house/page-4/');
					}


					resetExpandables(".expandable");
				});

				function resetExpandables(selectorVal) {
					/*  */

					$(selectorVal).each(function(index) {
					var slideHeight = 250;
					    if ($(selectorVal).attr('class').split(' ')[index]=='heroRegionContent'){
					    		slideHeight=103;
					    };
					    var $this = $(this);
					    var $wrap = $this.children(".wrap");
					    var defHeight = $wrap.height();
					    if (defHeight >= slideHeight) {
					        var $readMore = $this.find(".read-more");
					        $wrap.css("height", slideHeight + "px");
					        $readMore.append("<a href='#'>More +</a>");
					        $readMore.children("a").bind("click", function(event) {
					            var curHeight = $wrap.height();
					            if (curHeight == slideHeight) {
					                $wrap.animate({
					                    height: defHeight
					                }, "normal");
					                $(this).text("Less -");
					                $readMore.children(".elipses").hide();
					                // $wrap.children(".gradient").fadeOut();
					            } else {
					                $wrap.animate({
					                    height: slideHeight
					                }, "normal");
					                $(this).text("More +");
					                $readMore.children(".elipses").show();
					                // $wrap.children(".gradient").fadeIn();
					            }
					            return false;
					        });
					    } else {
					    	$this.find(".read-more").hide();
					    }
					});

				}


			</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
					// SearchBar Stick Top Nav
					var stickyNavTop;
					$(document).ready(function() {
						if( $('.search-nav').length ){
							updateStickyNavTop();
							var stickyNav = function(){
								var scrollTop = $(window).scrollTop();
								if (scrollTop > stickyNavTop) { $('.search-nav').addClass('sticky'); }
								else { $('.search-nav').removeClass('sticky'); }
							};
							stickyNav();
							$(window).scroll(function() { stickyNav(); });
						}

					});

					function updateStickyNavTop() {
						stickyNavTop = $('.search-nav').offset().top;
					}
					// ** Sticky top nav for the search bar

						e.preventDefault();
						$(this).tab('show');
